 Udagram is a simple cloud application developed alongside the Udacity Cloud Engineering Nanodegree. It allows users to register and log into a web client, post photos to the feed, and process photos using an image filtering microservice.[m
 [m
 The project is split into three parts:[m
[31m-1. [The Simple Frontend](https://github.com/udacity/cloud-developer/tree/master/course-02/exercises/udacity-c2-frontend)[m
[32m+[m[32m1. [The Simple Frontend](https://github.com/lasz-buis/cloud-developer/tree/master/course-02/exercises/udacity-c2-frontend)[m
 A basic Ionic client web application which consumes the RestAPI Backend. [Covered in the course][m
[31m-2. [The RestAPI Backend](https://github.com/udacity/cloud-developer/tree/master/course-02/exercises/udacity-c2-restapi), a Node-Express server which can be deployed to a cloud service. [Covered in the course][m
[31m-3. [The Image Filtering Microservice](https://github.com/udacity/cloud-developer/tree/master/course-02/project/image-filter-starter-code), the final project for the course. It is a Node-Express application which runs a simple script to process images. [Your assignment][m

[32m+[m[32mimport {decode} from 'jsonwebtoken'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport {JwtToken} from './JwtToken'[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/**[m
[32m+[m[32m * parse a JWT token and return a user id[m
[32m+[m[32m * @param jwtToken JWT token to parse[m
[32m+[m[32m * @returns a user id from JWT token[m
[32m+[m[32m */[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mexport function getUserId(jwtToken: string): string {[m
[32m+[m[32m    const decodedJwt = decode(jwtToken) as JwtToken[m
[32m+[m[32m    return decodedJwt.sub;[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfunction verifyToken (authHeader : string, secret: string):JwtToken[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    if (!authHeader)[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        throw new Error ('No authorization header');[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if (!authHeader.toLocaleLowerCase().startsWith('bearer '))[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        throw new Error ('Invalid authorization header');[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    const split = authHeader.split(' ');[m
[32m+[m[32m    const token = split [1];[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m   return verify (token, secret) as JwtToken;[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[32m+[m[32mexport const handler = middy( async (event: CustomAuthorizerEvent,[m
[32m+[m[32m                                     context): Promise<CustomAuthorizerResult> =>[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m

[32m+[m[32m                                          context.AUTH0_SECRET[secretField]);[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log('User was authorised');[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        return {[m
[32m+[m[32m            principalId: decodedToken.sub,[m
[32m+[m[32m            policyDocument: {[m
[32m+[m[32m                Version: '2012-10-17',[m
[32m+[m[32m                Statement: [[m
[32m+[m[32m                    {[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Action: 'execute-api:Invoke',[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Effect: 'Allow',[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Resource: '*'[m
[32m+[m[32m                    }[m
[32m+[m[32m                ][m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }catch (e){[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log ('User was not authorized', e.message);[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        return {[m
[32m+[m[32m            principalId: 'user',[m
[32m+[m[32m            policyDocument:{[m
[32m+[m[32m                Version: '2012-10-17',[m

[32m+[m[32m                    {[m

[32m+[m[32m});[m

[32m+[m[32mexport const handler = async (event: CustomAuthorizerEvent) : Promise<CustomAuthorizerResult> =>[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    try[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        const decodedToken = verifyToken( event.authorizationToken,[m
[32m+[m[32m                                          cert);[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log('User was authorised');[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        return {[m
[32m+[m[32m            principalId: decodedToken.sub,[m
[32m+[m[32m            policyDocument: {[m
[32m+[m[32m                Version: '2012-10-17',[m
[32m+[m[32m                Statement: [[m
[32m+[m[32m                    {[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Action: 'execute-api:Invoke',[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Effect: 'Allow',[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Resource: '*'[m
[32m+[m[32m                    }[m
[32m+[m[32m                ][m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }catch (e){[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log ('User was not authorized', e.message);[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        return {[m
[32m+[m[32m            principalId: 'user',[m
[32m+[m[32m            policyDocument:{[m
[32m+[m[32m                Version: '2012-10-17',[m
[32m+[m[32m                Statement: [[m
[32m+[m[32m                    {[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Action: 'execute-api:Invoke',[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Effect: 'Deny',[m
[32m+[m[32m                        Resource: '*'[m
[32m+[m[32m                    }[m
[32m+[m[32m                ][m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    return null;[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfunction verifyToken (authHeader : string, secret: string):JwtToken[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    if (!authHeader)[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        throw new Error ('No authorization header');[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if (!authHeader.toLocaleLowerCase().startsWith('bearer '))[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        throw new Error ('Invalid authorization header');[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    const split = authHeader.split(' ');[m
[32m+[m[32m    const token = split [1];[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m   return verify (  token,[m[41m [m
[32m+[m[32m                    secret,[m[41m [m
[32m+[m[32m                    {[m[41m [m
[32m+[m[32m                        algorithms: ['RS256'][m[41m [m
[32m+[m[32m                    }) as JwtToken[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[36m@@ -0,0 +1,50 @@[m
[32m+[m[32mimport {SNSEvent, S3EventRecord, SNSHandler} from 'aws-lambda'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport 'source-map-support/register'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport * as AWS from 'aws-sdk'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport * as Jimp from 'jimp/es'[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mconst s3 = new AWS.S3();[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mconst imagesBucketName = process.env.IMAGE_S3_BUCKET;[m
[32m+[m[32mconst thumbnailBucketName = process.env.THUMBNAILS_S3_BUCKET;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mexport const handler: SNSHandler = async (event: SNSEvent)=>[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    console.log('Processing SNS event ', JSON.stringify(event))[m
[32m+[m[32m    for (const snsRecord of event.Records)[m[41m [m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m      const s3EventStr = snsRecord.Sns.Message[m
[32m+[m[32m      console.log('Processing S3 event', s3EventStr)[m
[32m+[m[32m      const s3Event = JSON.parse(s3EventStr)[m
[32m+[m[41m  [m
[32m+[m[32m      for (const record of s3Event.Records) {[m
[32m+[m[32m        // "record" is an instance of S3EventRecord[m
[32m+[m[32m        await processImage(record) // A function that should resize each image[m
[32m+[m[32m      }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32masync function processImage (record: S3EventRecord)[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    const key = record.s3.object.key;[m
[32m+[m[32m    const response = await s3.getObject({[m
[32m+[m[32m      Bucket: imagesBucketName,[m
[32m+[m[32m      Key: key[m
[32m+[m[32m    }).promise()[m
[32m+[m[41m  [m
[32m+[m[32m    const body = response.Body;[m
[32m+[m[32m    // Read an image with the Jimp library[m
[32m+[m[32m    const image = await Jimp.read(body)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    // Resize an image maintaining the ratio between the image's width and height[m
[32m+[m[32m    image.resize(150, Jimp.AUTO)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    // Convert an image to a buffer that we can write to a different bucket[m
[32m+[m[32m    const convertedBuffer = await image.getBufferAsync(Jimp.AUTO)[m[41m [m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    await s3.putObject({[m
[32m+[m[32m        Bucket: thumbnailBucketName,[m
[32m+[m[32m        Key: `${key}.jpeg`,[m
[32m+[m[32m        Body: convertedBuffer[m
[32m+[m[32m    }).promise();[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[1m+++ b/course-04/temp-work/src/lambda/s3/sendNotification.ts[m
[36m@@ -0,0 +1,73 @@[m
[32m+[m[32mimport {SNSEvent, S3Event, SNSHandler} from 'aws-lambda'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport 'source-map-support/register'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport * as AWS from 'aws-sdk'[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mconst docClient = new AWS.DynamoDB.DocumentClient();[m
[32m+[m[32mconst connectionsTable = process.env.CONNECTIONS_TABLE;[m
[32m+[m[32mconst stage = process.env.STAGE;[m
[32m+[m[32mconst apiId = process.env.API_ID;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mconst connectionParams = {[m
[32m+[m[32m    apiVersion: "2018-11-29",[m
[32m+[m[32m    endpoint: `${apiId}.execute-api.us-west-2.amazonaws.con/${stage}`[m[41m    [m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mconst apiGateway = new AWS.ApiGatewayManagementApi (connectionParams);[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mexport const handler: SNSHandler = async (event: SNSEvent) =>[m[41m [m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    console.log ('Processing SNS event', JSON.stringify(event));[m
[32m+[m[32m    for (const snsRecord of event.Records)[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        const s3EventStr = snsRecord.Sns.Message;[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log ('Processing S3 event', s3EventStr);[m
[32m+[m[32m        const s3Event = JSON.parse (s3EventStr);[m
[32m+[m[32m        await processS3Event (s3Event);[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32masync function processS3Event (s3Event: S3Event)[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    for (const record of s3Event.Records)[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        const key = record.s3.object.key;[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log ('Processing S3 item with key: ', key);[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        const connections = await docClient.scan ({[m
[32m+[m[32m            TableName: connectionsTable[m
[32m+[m[32m            }).promise();[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        const payload = {[m
[32m+[m[32m            imageId: key[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        for (const connection of connections.Items)[m
[32m+[m[32m        {[m
[32m+[m[32m            const connectionId = connection.id;[m
[32m+[m[32m            await sendMessageToClient (connectionId, payload);[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32masync function sendMessageToClient (connectionId, payload)[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    try {[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log ('Sending message to a connection', connectionId);[m
[32m+[m[32m        await apiGateway.postToConnection ({[m
[32m+[m[32m            ConnectionId: connectionId,[m
[32m+[m[32m            Data: JSON.stringify(payload)[m
[32m+[m[32m        }).promise();[m
[32m+[m[32m    }catch (e)[m
[32m+[m[32m    {[m
[32m+[m[32m        console.log ('Falied to send message', JSON.stringify(e))[m
[32m+[m[32m        if (e.statusCode === 410)[m
[32m+[m[32m        {[m
[32m+[m[32m            console.log ('Stale connection');[m
[32m+[m[32m            await docClient.delete ({TableName: connectionsTable,[m
[32m+[m[32m            Key: {[m
[32m+[m[32m                id: connectionId[m
[32m+[m[32m            }}).promise();[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[32m+[m[32mimport 'source-map-support/register'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport * as AWS from 'aws-sdk'[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mconst docClient = new AWS.DynamoDB.DocumentClient();[m
[32m+[m[32mconst connectionsTable = process.env.CONNECTIONS_TABLE;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mexport const handler: APIGatewayProxyHandler = async (event: APIGatewayProxyEvent) : Promise<APIGatewayProxyResult> =>[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m    console.log ('Websocket connect', event);[m
[32m+[m[32m    const connectionId = event.requestContext.connectionId;[m
[32m+[m[32m    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();[m
[32m+[m[32m    const item = {[m

[32m+[m[32m        timestamp[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    await docClient.put ({[m
[32m+[m[32m        TableName: connectionsTable,[m
[32m+[m[32m        Item: item[m
[32m+[m[32m    }).promise();[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    return {[m
[32m+[m[32m        statusCode: 200,[m
[32m+[m[32m        body: ''[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
